        <a href="/wiki/Principality_of_Montenegro" title="Principality of Montenegro">
         Montenegro
        </a>
        declares its independence. Recognized in 1878 at the
        <a href="/wiki/Congress_of_Berlin" title="Congress of Berlin">
         Congress of Berlin
        </a>
        . Voluntarily united with
        <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Serbia" title="Kingdom of Serbia">
         Serbia
        </a>
        as
        <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Yugoslavia" title="Kingdom of Yugoslavia">
         Yugoslavia
        </a>
        in 1918.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th>
        1864
       </th>
       <td>
        <a href="/wiki/Great_Britain" title="Great Britain">
         Great Britain
        </a>
       </td>
       <td>
        The
        <a href="/wiki/United_States_of_the_Ionian_Islands" title="United States of the Ionian Islands">
         United States of the Ionian Islands
        </a>
        , a majority Greek protectorate, peaceably united with
        <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Greece" title="Kingdom of Greece">
         modern Greece
        </a>
        by the
        <a href="/wiki/Treaty_of_London_(1864)" title="Treaty of London (1864)">
         Treaty of London
        </a>
        .
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th>
        1865
       </th>
       <td>
        Spain
       </td>
       <td>
        <a href="/wiki/Captaincy_General_of_Santo_Domingo" title="Captaincy General of Santo Domingo">
         Santo Domingo
        </a>
        regains independence as the
        <a href="/wiki/Dominican_Republic" title="Dominican Republic">
         Dominican Republic
        </a>
        after four years as a restored colony.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th>
        1867
       </th>
       <td>
        Russia
       </td>
       <td>
        The
        <a href="/wiki/Russian_Empire" title="Russian Empire">
         Russian Empire
        </a>
        sells
        <a href="/wiki/Russian_America" title="Russian America">
         Alaska
        </a>
        to the United States for $7.2 million. Attained statehood on January 3, 1959.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th>
        1867
       </th>
       <td>
        <a href="/wiki/Great_Britain" title="Great Britain">
         Great Britain
        </a>
       </td>
       <td>
        The United Kingdom grants autonomy to Canada. This is popularly considered Canada's independence day, but Britain retained legal powers over Canada until 1931, and a role in Canada constitutional law until 1982.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th>
        1868
       </th>
       <td>
        Spain
       </td>
       <td>
        <a href="/wiki/Captaincy_General_of_Cuba" title="Captaincy General of Cuba">
         Cuba
        </a>
        briefly declares itself independent before being reconquered.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th>
        1869
       </th>
       <td>
        <a href="/wiki/Ottoman_Empire" title="Ottoman Empire">
         Ottoman Empire
        </a>
       </td>
       <td>
        <a href="/wiki/Principality_of_Serbia" title="Principality of Serbia">
         Serbia
        </a>
        declares its full independence from the Ottoman Empire. Recognized in 1878 at the
        <a href="/wiki/Congress_of_Berlin" title="Congress of Berlin">
         Congress of Berlin
        </a>
        . Renamed
        <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Yugoslavia" title="Kingdom of Yugoslavia">
         Yugoslavia
        </a>
        in 1918.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th>
        1877
       </th>
       <td>
        <a href="/wiki/Ottoman_Empire" title="Ottoman Empire">
         Ottoman Empire
        </a>
       </td>
       <td>
        The
        <a href="/wiki/Danubian_Principalities" title="Danubian Principalities">
         United Principalities of Romania
        </a>
        declare their independence. Recognized in 1878 at the
        <a href="/wiki/Congress_of_Berlin" title="Congress of Berlin">
         Congress of Berlin
        </a>
        .
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th>
        1898
       </th>
       <td>
        Spain
       </td>
       <td>
        The United States (barred from annexing
        <a href="/wiki/Captaincy_General_of_Cuba" title="Captaincy General of Cuba">
         Cuba
        </a>
        itself by the
        <a href="/wiki/Teller_Amendment" title="Teller Amendment">
         Teller Amendment
        </a>
        ) forces Spain to abjure its own claims to the island in the
        <a href="/wiki/Treaty_of_Paris_(1898)" title="Treaty of Paris (1898)">
         Treaty of Paris
        </a>
        ending the
        <a href="/wiki/Spanish%E2%80%93American_War" title="SpanishAmerican War">
         SpanishAmerican War
        </a>
        . Various other Spanish colonies are purchased for $20 million, including the Philippines, which are granted independence in 1934.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th>
        1902
       </th>
       <td>
        United States
       </td>
       <td>
        Cuba granted independence.
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Guantanamo_Bay" title="Guantanamo Bay">
         Guantanamo Bay
        </a>
        is leased in perpetuity as a
        <a href="/wiki/United_States_Navy" title="United States Navy">
         US Naval base
        </a>
        .
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th>
        1908
       </th>
       <td>
        <a href="/wiki/Ottoman_Empire" title="Ottoman Empire">
         Ottoman Empire
        </a>
       </td>
       <td>
        <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Bulgaria" title="Kingdom of Bulgaria">
         Bulgaria
        </a>
        , largely autonomous since the Congress of Berlin, declares itself fully independent of the
        <a href="/wiki/Ottoman_Empire" title="Ottoman Empire">
         Ottoman Empire
        </a>
        .
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th>
        1912
       </th>
       <td>
        <a href="/wiki/Ottoman_Empire" title="Ottoman Empire">
         Ottoman Empire
        </a>
       </td>
       <td>
        <a href="/wiki/Albania" title="Albania">
         Albania
        </a>
        declares independence. Recognized in the 1913
        <a href="/wiki/Treaty_of_London_(1913)" title="Treaty of London (1913)">
         Treaty of London
        </a>
        .
       </td>
      </tr>
     </table>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Inter-War_Period">
       Inter-War Period
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=Decolonization&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Inter-War Period">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <table class="wikitable">
      <tr style="background-color:#E9E9E9">
       <th>
        Year
       </th>
       <th>
        Colonizer
       </th>
       <th>
        Event
       </th>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th>
        1916
       </th>
       <td>
        <a href="/wiki/Russian_Empire" title="Russian Empire">
         Russian Empire
        </a>
       </td>
       <td>
        The independence of
        <a href="/wiki/Congress_Poland" title="Congress Poland">
         Russian Poland
        </a>
        as a
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Poland_(1916%E2%80%931918)" title="Kingdom of Poland (19161918)">
         new kingdom
        </a>
        is proclaimed by occupying
        <a href="/wiki/German_Empire" title="German Empire">
         German
        </a>
        and
        <a href="/wiki/Austria-Hungary" title="Austria-Hungary">
         Austro-Hungarian
        </a>
        forces. Recognized by
        <a href="/wiki/Russian_Soviet_Federative_Socialist_Republic" title="Russian Soviet Federative Socialist Republic">
         Soviet Russia
        </a>
        in the 1918
        <a href="/wiki/Treaty_of_Brest-Litovsk" title="Treaty of Brest-Litovsk">
         Treaty of Brest-Litovsk
        </a>
        . Absorbed Polish regions from Germany, Austria, and Hungary following
        <a href="/wiki/World_War_I" title="World War I">
         World War I
        </a>
        and from Soviet Russia and
        <a href="/wiki/Ukrainian_Soviet_Socialist_Republic" title="Ukrainian Soviet Socialist Republic">
         Soviet Ukraine
        </a>
        after the
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Polish-Soviet_War" title="Polish-Soviet War">
         Polish-Soviet War
        </a>
        .
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th>
        1917
       </th>
       <td>
        <a href="/wiki/Russian_Empire" title="Russian Empire">
         Russian Empire
        </a>
       </td>
       <td>
        Finland declares its independence. Recognized in the 1918
        <a href="/wiki/Treaty_of_Brest-Litovsk" title="Treaty of Brest-Litovsk">
         Treaty of Brest-Litovsk
        </a>
        , although
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Karelian_question_in_Finnish_politics" title="Karelian question in Finnish politics">
         Karelia remained disputed
        </a>
        .
        <a href="/wiki/Crimean_People%27s_Republic" title="Crimean People's Republic">
         Crimean People's Republic
        </a>
        declares independence but Crimean Tatar forces hold out less than a month against the Bolsheviks. Wolga Tatars declare independence of the
        <a href="/wiki/Idel-Ural_State" title="Idel-Ural State">
         Idel-Ural State
        </a>
        , other ethnic groups including
        <a href="/wiki/Volga_Germans" title="Volga Germans">
         Volga Germans
        </a>
        join them. Kazaks declare independence of the
        <a href="/wiki/Alash_Autonomy" title="Alash Autonomy">
         Alash Autonomy
        </a>
        .
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th rowspan="3">
        1918
       </th>
       <td>
        <a href="/wiki/Russian_Empire" title="Russian Empire">
         Russian Empire
        </a>
       </td>
       <td>
        <a href="/wiki/Azerbaijan_Democratic_Republic" title="Azerbaijan Democratic Republic">
         Azerbaijan Democratic Republic
        </a>
        ,
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Republic_of_Georgia" title="Republic of Georgia">
         Republic of Georgia
        </a>
        and
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Republic_of_Armenia" title="Republic of Armenia">
         Republic of Armenia
        </a>
        declare independence on May 2628. Occupied by the Soviet Russia in 1920-1921.
        <a href="/wiki/Estonia" title="Estonia">
         Estonia
        </a>
        ,
        <a href="/wiki/Latvia" title="Latvia">
         Latvia
        </a>
        and Lithuania also declare independence. Occupied by the
        <a href="/wiki/Soviet_Union" title="Soviet Union">
         Soviet Union
        </a>
        from 1940 to 1991.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td rowspan="2">
        <a href="/wiki/Austria-Hungary" title="Austria-Hungary">
         Austria-Hungary
        </a>
       </td>
       <td>
        <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Bohemia" title="Kingdom of Bohemia">
         Bohemia
        </a>
        ,
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/March_of_Moravia" title="March of Moravia">
         Moravia
        </a>
        , and sections of
        <a href="/wiki/Czech_Silesia" title="Czech Silesia">
         Silesia
        </a>
        ,
        <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Galicia_and_Lodomeria" title="Kingdom of Galicia and Lodomeria">
         Galicia
        </a>
        , and
        <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Hungary" title="Kingdom of Hungary">
         Hungary
        </a>
        declare their independence as
        <a href="/wiki/Czechoslovakia" title="Czechoslovakia">
         Czechoslovakia
        </a>
        . Recognized in the
        <a href="/wiki/Treaty_of_Trianon" title="Treaty of Trianon">
         Treaty of Trianon
        </a>
        in 1920.
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Slovak_Republic_(1939%E2%80%931945)" title="Slovak Republic (19391945)">
         Slovakia
        </a>
        independent from 1939 to 1945.
        <a href="/wiki/Carpatho-Ukraine" title="Carpatho-Ukraine">
         Carpathian Ruthenia
        </a>
        independent in 1939, eventually annexed to
        <a href="/wiki/Ukrainian_Soviet_Socialist_Republic" title="Ukrainian Soviet Socialist Republic">
         Ukraine
        </a>
        . Secession of
        <a href="/wiki/Slovakia" title="Slovakia">
         Slovakia
        </a>
        in 1993.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Croatia-Slavonia" title="Kingdom of Croatia-Slavonia">
         Croatia-Slavonia
        </a>
        and
        <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Dalmatia" title="Kingdom of Dalmatia">
         Dalmatia
        </a>
        declare their independence as the
        <a href="/wiki/State_of_Slovenes,_Croats_and_Serbs" title="State of Slovenes, Croats and Serbs">
         State of Slovenes, Croats and Serbs
        </a>
        and swiftly unites with
        <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Serbia" title="Kingdom of Serbia">
         Serbia
        </a>
        as the
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Serbs,_Croats_and_Slovenes" title="Kingdom of Serbs, Croats and Slovenes">
         Kingdom of Serbs, Croats and Slovenes
        </a>
        which later became
        <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Yugoslavia" title="Kingdom of Yugoslavia">
         Yugoslavia
        </a>
        .
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th>
        1919
       </th>
       <td>
        United Kingdom
       </td>
       <td>
        End of the
        <a href="/wiki/Protectorate" title="Protectorate">
         protectorate
        </a>
        over
        <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">
         Afghanistan
        </a>
        , when the United Kingdom accepts the presence of a Soviet ambassador in Kabul.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th>
        1921
       </th>
       <td>
        China
       </td>
       <td>
        Communist Mongolian revolutionaries, with the help of the
        <a href="/wiki/Red_Army" title="Red Army">
         Red Army
        </a>
        , expel the Chinese government presence from
        <a href="/wiki/Outer_Mongolia" title="Outer Mongolia">
         Outer Mongolia
        </a>
        , and Mongolia passes into the heavy influence of the
        <a href="/wiki/Soviet_Union" title="Soviet Union">
         Soviet Union
        </a>
        . Mongolia was recognized by the
        <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">
         United Nations
        </a>
        in 1961.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th rowspan="2">
        1922
       </th>
       <td rowspan="2">
        United Kingdom
       </td>
       <td>
        In Ireland, following insurgency by the
        <a href="/wiki/Irish_Republican_Army" title="Irish Republican Army">
         Irish Republican Army
        </a>
        , most of Ireland separates from the United Kingdom as the
        <a href="/wiki/Irish_Free_State" title="Irish Free State">
         Irish Free State
        </a>
        , remaining as a
        <a href="/wiki/Dominion" title="Dominion">
         dominion
        </a>
        .
        <a href="/wiki/Northern_Ireland" title="Northern Ireland">
         Northern Ireland
        </a>
        , the north-east area of the island, remains within the United Kingdom.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        Egypt is
        <a href="/wiki/Unilateral_Declaration_of_Egyptian_Independence" title="Unilateral Declaration of Egyptian Independence">
         unilaterally granted independence
        </a>
        by the United Kingdom. However, four matters (imperial communications, defence, the protection of foreign interests and minorities, as well as
        <a href="/wiki/Anglo-Egyptian_Sudan" title="Anglo-Egyptian Sudan">
         Sudan
        </a>
        ) remain "absolutely reserved to the discretion" of the British government, which greatly restricts the full exercise of Egyptian sovereignty.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th>
        1923
       </th>
       <td>
        United Kingdom
       </td>
       <td>
        End of the
        <i>
         de facto
        </i>
        protectorate over
        <a href="/wiki/Nepal" title="Nepal">
         Nepal
        </a>
        which was never truly colonized.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th>
        1930
       </th>
       <td>
        United Kingdom
       </td>
       <td>
        The United Kingdom returns the leased port territory at
        <a href="/wiki/Weihai" title="Weihai">
         Weihaiwei
        </a>
        to China, the first episode of decolonisation in East Asia.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th>
        1931
       </th>
       <td>
        United Kingdom
       </td>
       <td>
        The
        <a href="/wiki/Statute_of_Westminster_1931" title="Statute of Westminster 1931">
         Statute of Westminster
        </a>
        grants virtually full independence to Canada, the
        <a href="/wiki/Irish_Free_State" title="Irish Free State">
         Irish Free State
        </a>
        , and the and the
        <a href="/wiki/Union_of_South_Africa" title="Union of South Africa">
         Union of South Africa
        </a>
        when it declares the
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/British_parliament" title="British parliament">
         British parliament
        </a>
        incapable of passing law over these former colonies without their own consent. Doesn't take effect over New Zealand,
        <a href="/wiki/Newfoundland_and_Labrador" title="Newfoundland and Labrador">
         Newfoundland
        </a>
        , and the Commonwealth of Australia, until independently ratified by these dominions.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th>
        1932
       </th>
       <td>
        United Kingdom
       </td>
       <td>
        Ends
        <a href="/wiki/League_of_Nations" title="League of Nations">
         League of Nations
        </a>
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/British_Mandate_of_Mesopotamia" title="British Mandate of Mesopotamia">
         Mandate
        </a>
        over
        <a href="/wiki/Iraq" title="Iraq">
         Iraq
        </a>
        . The United Kingdom continues to station troops in the country and influence the Iraqi government until 1958.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th>
        1934
       </th>
       <td>
        United States
       </td>
       <td>
        Establishes the
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Philippine_Islands" title="Philippine Islands">
         Philippine Islands
        </a>
        into a
        <a href="/wiki/Commonwealth_of_the_Philippines" title="Commonwealth of the Philippines">
         Commonwealth
        </a>
        under the provisions of the
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Philippine_Independence_Act" title="Philippine Independence Act">
         Philippine Independence Act
        </a>
        . Abrogates
        <a href="/wiki/Platt_Amendment" title="Platt Amendment">
         Platt Amendment
        </a>
        , which gave it direct authority to intervene in Cuba.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th>
        1941
       </th>
       <td>
        France
       </td>
       <td>
        <a href="/wiki/Lebanon" title="Lebanon">
         Lebanon
        </a>
        declares independence, effectively ending the French mandate (previously together with Syria) - it is recognized in 1943.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th>
        1941
       </th>
       <td>
        Italy
       </td>
       <td>
        <a href="/wiki/Ethiopia" title="Ethiopia">
         Ethiopia
        </a>
        ,
        <a href="/wiki/Eritrea" title="Eritrea">
         Eritrea
        </a>
        and
        <a href="/wiki/Tigray_Province" title="Tigray Province">
         Tigray Province
        </a>
        (appended to it), and
        <a href="/wiki/Italian_Somaliland" title="Italian Somaliland">
         Italian Somaliland
        </a>
        are taken by
        <a href="/wiki/Allies_of_World_War_II" title="Allies of World War II">
         the Allies
        </a>
        after an uneasy occupation of Ethiopia since 1935-36, and no longer joined as one colonial federal state; the
        <a href="/wiki/Ogaden" title="Ogaden">
         Ogaden
        </a>
        desert (disputed by
        <a href="/wiki/Somalia" title="Somalia">
         Somalia
        </a>
        ) remains under British military control until 1948.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th>
        1942
       </th>
       <td>
        United Kingdom
       </td>
       <td>
        Australia ratifies the Statute of Westminster.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th>
        1944
       </th>
       <td>
        Denmark
       </td>
       <td>
        Following a
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Plebiscite" title="Plebiscite">
         plebiscite
        </a>
        ,
        <a href="/wiki/Iceland" title="Iceland">
         Iceland
        </a>
        formally becomes an independent republic on June 17, 1944.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th rowspan="5">
        1945
       </th>
       <td rowspan="2">
        Japan
       </td>
       <td>
        After surrender of Japan, Korea is occupied by the
        <a href="/wiki/Soviet_Union" title="Soviet Union">
         Soviet Union
        </a>
        and the United States.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        After surrender of Japan,
        <a href="/wiki/Mengjiang" title="Mengjiang">
         Mengjiang
        </a>
        ,
        <a href="/wiki/Manchukuo" title="Manchukuo">
         Manchukuo
        </a>
        and Taiwan are returned to China.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        France
       </td>
       <td>
        Vietnam declares independence, but France does not recognize it until 1954.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        Netherlands
       </td>
       <td>
        Indonesia declares independence, which the Netherlands does not recognize until December 1949.
       </td>

     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Cold_War">
       Cold War
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=Decolonization&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Cold War">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <table class="wikitable">
      <tr style="background-color:#E9E9E9">
       <th>
        Year
       </th>
       <th>
        Colonizer
       </th>
       <th>
        Event
       </th>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th rowspan="3">
        1946
       </th>
       <td>
        United States
       </td>
       <td>
        The
        <a href="/wiki/Treaty_of_Manila_(1946)" title="Treaty of Manila (1946)">
         treaty of Manila
        </a>
        is signed, effectively ending over 380 years of foreign domination in the Philippines.
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_military" title="United States military">
         United States military
        </a>
        bases continued to be stationed in the islands.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        United Kingdom
       </td>
       <td>
        The former emirate of Transjordan (present-day
        <a href="/wiki/Jordan" title="Jordan">
         Jordan
        </a>
        ) becomes an independent
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hashemite" title="Hashemite">
         Hashemite
        </a>
        kingdom when the United Kingdom relinquishes
        <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">
         UN
        </a>
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_Nations_Trusteeship" title="United Nations Trusteeship">
         trusteeship
        </a>

       </th>
       <td>
        United Kingdom
       </td>
       <td>
        <a href="/wiki/Grenada" title="Grenada">
         Grenada
        </a>
        in the
        <a href="/wiki/Caribbean" title="Caribbean">
         Caribbean
        </a>
        becomes independent.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        Portugal
       </td>
       <td>
        <a href="/wiki/Guinea-Bissau" title="Guinea-Bissau">
         Guinea-Bissau
        </a>
        on the coast of West-Africa is recognized as independent by Portugal.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        United States
       </td>
       <td>
        The
        <a href="/wiki/Laurel%E2%80%93Langley_Agreement" title="LaurelLangley Agreement">
         LaurelLangley Agreement
        </a>
        is repealed by
        <a href="/wiki/Ferdinand_Marcos" title="Ferdinand Marcos">
         Ferdinand Marcos
        </a>
        .
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th rowspan="4">
        1975
       </th>
       <td>
        France
       </td>
       <td>
        The
        <a href="/wiki/Comoros" title="Comoros">
         Comoros
        </a>
        archipelago in the Indian Ocean off the coast of Africa is granted independence.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        Portugal
       </td>
       <td>
        <a href="/wiki/Angola" title="Angola">
         Angola
        </a>
        ,
        <a href="/wiki/Mozambique" title="Mozambique">
         Mozambique
        </a>
        and the island groups of
        <a href="/wiki/Cape_Verde" title="Cape Verde">
         Cape Verde
        </a>
        and
        <a href="/wiki/S%C3%A3o_Tom%C3%A9_and_Pr%C3%ADncipe" title="So Tom and Prncipe">
         So Tom and Prncipe
        </a>
        , all four in Africa, achieve independence.
        <a href="/wiki/East_Timor" title="East Timor">
         East Timor
        </a>
        declares independence, but is subsequently occupied and annexed by Indonesia nine days later.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        Netherlands
       </td>
       <td>
        <a href="/wiki/Suriname" title="Suriname">
         Suriname
        </a>
        (then Dutch Guiana) becomes independent.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        Australia
       </td>
       <td>
        Released from trusteeship,
        <a href="/wiki/Papua_New_Guinea" title="Papua New Guinea">
         Papua New Guinea
        </a>
        gains independence.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th rowspan="2">
        1976
       </th>
       <td>
        United Kingdom
       </td>
       <td>
        <a href="/wiki/Seychelles" title="Seychelles">
         Seychelles
        </a>
        archipelago in the Indian Ocean off the African coast becomes independent (one year after granting of self-rule).
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        Spain
       </td>
       <td>
        The Spanish colonial rule de facto terminated over the
        <a href="/wiki/Western_Sahara" title="Western Sahara">
         Western Sahara
        </a>
        (then Rio de Oro), when the territory was passed on to and partitioned between
        <a href="/wiki/Mauritania" title="Mauritania">
         Mauritania
        </a>
        and
        <a href="/wiki/Morocco" title="Morocco">
         Morocco
        </a>
        (which annexes the entire territory in 1979), rendering the declared independence of the
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Saharawi_Arab_Democratic_Republic" title="Saharawi Arab Democratic Republic">
         Saharawi Arab Democratic Republic
        </a>
        ineffective to the present day.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th>
        1977
       </th>
       <td>
        France
       </td>
       <td>
        <a href="/wiki/French_Somaliland" title="French Somaliland">
         French Somaliland
        </a>
        , also known as the "
        <a href="/wiki/French_Territory_of_the_Afars_and_the_Issas" title="French Territory of the Afars and the Issas">
         French Territory of the Afars and the Issas
        </a>
        " (after its dominant ethnic groups), the present
        <a href="/wiki/Djibouti" title="Djibouti">
         Djibouti
        </a>
        , gains independence.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th>
        1978
       </th>
       <td>
        United Kingdom
       </td>
       <td>
        <a href="/wiki/Dominica" title="Dominica">
         Dominica
        </a>
        in the Caribbean and the
        <a href="/wiki/Solomon_Islands" title="Solomon Islands">
         Solomon Islands
        </a>
        , as well as
        <a href="/wiki/Tuvalu" title="Tuvalu">
         Tuvalu
        </a>
        (then the Ellice Islands), all in the South Sea, become independent.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th rowspan="2">
        1979
       </th>
       <td>
        United States
       </td>
       <td>
        Returns the
        <a href="/wiki/Panama_Canal_Zone" title="Panama Canal Zone">
         Panama Canal Zone
        </a>
        (held under a regime
        <i>
         sui generis
        </i>
        since 1903) to the republic of Panama.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td rowspan="7">
        United Kingdom
       </td>
       <td>
        The Gilbert Islands (present-day
        <a href="/wiki/Kiribati" title="Kiribati">
         Kiribati
        </a>
        ) in the South Sea as well as
        <a href="/wiki/Saint_Vincent_and_the_Grenadines" title="Saint Vincent and the Grenadines">
         Saint Vincent and the Grenadines
        </a>
        and
        <a href="/wiki/Saint_Lucia" title="Saint Lucia">
         Saint Lucia
        </a>
        in the Caribbean become independent.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th>
        1980
       </th>
       <td>
        <a href="/wiki/Zimbabwe" title="Zimbabwe">
         Zimbabwe
        </a>
        (then [Southern] Rhodesia), already independent
        <i>
         de facto
        </i>
        , becomes formally independent. The joint Anglo-French colony of the
        <a href="/wiki/New_Hebrides" title="New Hebrides">
         New Hebrides
        </a>
        becomes the independent island republic of
        <a href="/wiki/Vanuatu" title="Vanuatu">
         Vanuatu
        </a>
        .
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th>
        1981
       </th>
       <td>
        <a href="/wiki/Belize" title="Belize">
         Belize
        </a>
        (then British Honduras) and
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Antigua_%26_Barbuda" title="Antigua &amp; Barbuda">
         Antigua &amp; Barbuda
        </a>
        become independent.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th>
        1982
       </th>
       <td>
        Canada gains full independence from the British parliament with the
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Canada_Act" title="Canada Act">
         Canada Act
        </a>
        .
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th>
        1983
       </th>
       <td>
        <a href="/wiki/Saint_Kitts_and_Nevis" title="Saint Kitts and Nevis">
         Saint Kitts and Nevis
        </a>
        (an associated state since 1963) becomes independent.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th>
        1984
       </th>
       <td>
        <a href="/wiki/Brunei" title="Brunei">
         Brunei
        </a>
        sultanate on Borneo becomes independent.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th>
        1986
       </th>
       <td>
        Australia and New Zealand become fully independent with the
        <a href="/wiki/Australia_Act_1986" title="Australia Act 1986">
         Australia Act 1986
        </a>
        and The
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/New_Zealand_Constitution_Act_1986" title="New Zealand Constitution Act 1986">
         New Zealand Constitution Act 1986
        </a>
        .
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th rowspan="2">
        1990
       </th>
       <td>
        South Africa
       </td>
       <td>
        <a href="/wiki/Namibia" title="Namibia">
         Namibia
        </a>
        becomes independent from South Africa.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td>
        United States
       </td>
       <td>
        The
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/UN_Security_Council" title="UN Security Council">
         UN Security Council
        </a>
        gives final approval to end the
        <a href="/wiki/Trust_Territory_of_the_Pacific_Islands" title="Trust Territory of the Pacific Islands">
         U.S. Trust Territory of the Pacific
        </a>
        (dissolved already in 1986), finalizing the independence of the
        <a href="/wiki/Marshall_Islands" title="Marshall Islands">
         Marshall Islands
        </a>
        and the
        <a href="/wiki/Federated_States_of_Micronesia" title="Federated States of Micronesia">
         Federated States of Micronesia
        </a>
        , having been a colonial possession of the empire of Japan before UN trusteeship.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th>
        1991
       </th>
       <td>
        <a href="/wiki/Soviet_Union" title="Soviet Union">
         Soviet Union
        </a>
       </td>
       <td>
        <a href="/wiki/Estonia" title="Estonia">
         Estonia
        </a>
        ,
        <a href="/wiki/Latvia" title="Latvia">
         Latvia
        </a>
        , Lithuania,
        <a href="/wiki/Ukraine" title="Ukraine">
         Ukraine
        </a>
        ,
        <a href="/wiki/Belarus" title="Belarus">
         Belarus
        </a>
        ,
        <a href="/wiki/Moldova" title="Moldova">
         Moldova
        </a>
        ,
        <a href="/wiki/Armenia" title="Armenia">
         Armenia
        </a>
        ,
        <a href="/wiki/Georgia_(country)" title="Georgia (country)">
         Georgia
        </a>
        ,
        <a href="/wiki/Azerbaijan" title="Azerbaijan">
         Azerbaijan
        </a>
        ,
        <a href="/wiki/Kazakhstan" title="Kazakhstan">
         Kazakhstan
        </a>
        ,
        <a href="/wiki/Uzbekistan" title="Uzbekistan">
         Uzbekistan
        </a>
        ,
        <a href="/wiki/Tajikistan" title="Tajikistan">
         Tajikistan
        </a>
        ,
        <a href="/wiki/Kyrgyzstan" title="Kyrgyzstan">
         Kyrgyzstan
        </a>
        , Russia and
        <a href="/wiki/Turkmenistan" title="Turkmenistan">
         Turkmenistan
        </a>
        become independent from the Soviet Union.
       </td>
      </tr>
     </table>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Post.E2.80.93Cold_War_era">
       PostCold War era
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=Decolonization&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: PostCold War era">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h3>
     <table class="wikitable">
      <tr style="background-color:#E9E9E9">
       <th>
        Year
       </th>
       <th>
        Colonizer
       </th>
       <th>
        Event
       </th>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th>
        1991
       </th>
       <td>
        United States
       </td>
       <td>
        U.S. forces withdraw from
        <a href="/wiki/Subic_Bay" title="Subic Bay">
         Subic Bay
        </a>
        and
        <a href="/wiki/Clark_Air_Base" title="Clark Air Base">
         Clark Air Base
        </a>
        in the Philippines ending major
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/U.S._military" title="U.S. military">
         U.S. military
        </a>
        presence, which lasted for almost a century.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th>
        1993
       </th>
       <td>
        <a href="/wiki/Ethiopia" title="Ethiopia">
         Ethiopia
        </a>
       </td>
       <td>
        <a href="/wiki/Eritrea" title="Eritrea">
         Eritrea
        </a>
        , a former
        <a href="/wiki/Italy" title="Italy">
         Italian
        </a>
        colony declares independence and is subsequently recognized.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th>
        1994
       </th>
       <td>
        United States
       </td>
       <td>
        <a href="/wiki/Palau" title="Palau">
         Palau
        </a>
        (after a transitional period as a Republic since 1981, and before part of the
        <a href="/wiki/Trust_Territory_of_the_Pacific_Islands" title="Trust Territory of the Pacific Islands">
         U.S. Trust territory of the Pacific
        </a>
        ) becomes independent from its former trustee, having been a mandate of the Japanese Empire before UN trusteeship.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th>
        1997
       </th>
       <td>
        United Kingdom
       </td>
       <td>
        The
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/British_dependent_territory" title="British dependent territory">
         British dependent territory
        </a>
        of
        <a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong" title="Hong Kong">
         Hong Kong
        </a>
        is given to
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">
         People's Republic of China
        </a>
        .
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th>
        1999
       </th>
       <td>
        Portugal
       </td>
       <td>
        <a href="/wiki/Macau" title="Macau">
         Macau
        </a>
        is given to
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">
         People's Republic of China
        </a>
        . It is the last in a series of coastal enclaves that militarily stronger powers had obtained through treaties from the
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Qing_Empire" title="Qing Empire">
         Qing Empire
        </a>
        which ruled China. Macau, like Hong Kong, is not organized into the existing provincial structure applied to other provinces of the People's Republic of China, but is guaranteed an autonomous system of government within the People's Republic of China as a "Special Administrative Region" or S.A.R.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th>
        2002
       </th>
       <td>
        Indonesia
       </td>
       <td>
        <a href="/wiki/East_Timor" title="East Timor">
         East Timor
        </a>
        formally achieves independence after a transitional UN administration, three years after Indonesia ended its quarter-century occupation of the former Portuguese colony.
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th>
        2011
       </th>
       <td>
        <a href="/wiki/Sudan" title="Sudan">
         Sudan
        </a>
       </td>
       <td>
        <a href="/wiki/South_Sudan" title="South Sudan">
         South Sudan
        </a>
        formally achieves independence.
       </td>
      </tr>
     </table>

       </i>
       (2013)
       <a class="external text" href="http://www.amazon.com/The-Wind-Change-Decolonization-Post-Colonial/dp/023036103X" rel="nofollow">
        excerpt
       </a>
      </li>
      <li>

       <i>

       </i>
       (Routledge, 2014)

       <i>
        Critical Inquiry
       </i>
